	focus = {
		id = SPR_post_civil_war
		icon = GFX_goal_SPR_post_civil_war
		cost = 0
		relative_position_id = SPR_Crossroads_of_Chaos
		mutually_exclusive = {}
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = SPR_post_civil_war_tt
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = election_success
						NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war }
						NOT = { has_country_flag = aftermath_of_the_civil_war }
					}
					AND = {
						has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war
						NOT = { country_exists = CNT }
						NOT = { country_exists = CAR }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		x = 0
		y = 7
		offset = {
			y = 4
			trigger = {
				has_allied_with_anyone_republic = yes
			}
		}
		offset = {
			y = -6
			trigger = {
				has_allied_with_anyone_kingdom = yes
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		bypass = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = SPR_post_civil_war_tt
				has_country_flag = aftermath_of_the_civil_war
			}
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SPR_post_civil_war"
			custom_effect_tooltip = unlock_focuses
			hidden_effect = {
				SRR_civil_war_end_effect = yes
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL FOCUS_FILTER_STABILITY }
	}
